Its empirical leg was a single PARTIAL run (v4); last session's result/aann-inferential-v6 replicated the FC/NLI dissociation CELL FOR CELL on 40 fresh held-out items -- which EXERCISED the essay's own revision triggers (a) and (b) and FIRED NEITHER: (a) the powered replication did NOT show claude/gemini NLI converging (preference-without-commitment reading for those two CONFIRMED, not retracted), (b) the FC shift DID replicate (+0.875/+0.575/+0.90, antecedent STRENGTHENED not weakened). PHILOSOPHICAL HEADLINE: wrote the project's TWELFTH essay, essay/undischargeable-negative (methodological/philosophical; meaning-senses model-internal/functional-vs-formal/relational; status draft). Thesis (logical-epistemic backbone for the charter's "write the null" discipline): a capability POSITIVE is a verifiable EXISTENTIAL (one witness — one elicitation on which M succeeds — discharges it); a capability ABSENCE ("M cannot do X") is an unverifiable UNIVERSAL over elicitations no finite behavioral battery reaches → from behavior alone the negative is UNDISCHARGEABLE (the mirror of the Popperian law/existence asymmetry). This VINDICATES the null discipline (project nulls are instrument-relative facts, not capacity-absence claims; the only error is the silent upgrade to "M cannot"). Builds a TYPOLOGY of negatives — (1) effect-null under an instrument (relational-reference-game-v1 order-insensitivity; grounding redundancy), (2) instrument-uninterpretable / prerequisite-gate failure (gemini DIRECT 0.583 + gpt 0.194 UNINTERPRETABLE on Option C), (3) structural reach-closure (transcript ceiling — a negative about the INSTRUMENT's reach, not the model's capacity) — and keeps a 4th box (a BEHAVIORAL capability-absence) deliberately empty (only a non-behavioral architectural/mechanistic proof closes it; trigger a). Decision-relevant payoff: re-running a failing probe is futile (another ∀-instance, never the ∀); only a WITNESS-SEEKING probe (an easier elicitation = capability-split trigger b) or a structural argument can change a negative's status. GENERALIZES essay/capability-split (clean-null/instrument-uninterpretable mark, lifted split-panel→single-model) and lifts essay/transcript-ceiling's structural closure into "kind 3" (links depends-on both + concept/formal-vs-functional-competence + result/relational-order-composition-c + result/relational-reference-game-v1 + essay/rung-iv-instrument). NO new empirical claim, NO human comparison. PROCESS: orchestrator AUTHORED the essay (judgement-heavy; coheres with 4 existing essays → not parallelized per PROTOCOL §A); 1 INDEPENDENT read-only adversarial review agent over the essay + all 6 cited pages → 1 BLOCKER (quote "lacks order-sensitive composition in general" mis-cited to result/relational-order-composition-c — it lives on essay/capability-split; fixed by re-attributing, and citing the result page for "composition-ability limit, not a parse artifact" which originates there) + 3 SHOULD-FIX (chained-quote attribution; under-signposted reconciliation of kind-3 reach-closure vs trigger-a capacity-proof in the reporting box → named the off-typology "proof-closed absence" route explicitly; an "adequately-powered" overstatement contradicting the relational pilot's own "detects only large, consistent order effects" caveat → reworded to "limited and stated power" + added the pilot's verbatim hedge) — ALL applied; reviewer confirmed all other quotes verbatim, front-matter/link-relations/anchor discipline clean, and the essay's distinctness from the two essays it generalizes is real. 2026-06-19  single-unit(philosophical, 39th session). RECONCILE (PROTOCOL §2): wiki/decisions/open/ empty at cold start — NONE opened or ratified; no Tom override. Lean was due PHILOSOPHICAL (tracks ended ...emp(38)). HEADLINE: wrote the project's 15th essay, essay/output-channel-confound — the methodological lesson the 38th-session witness teaches, the unit the 38th handoff named ("the elicitation surface as a capability-masker"). NAMES A CONFOUND: the OUTPUT CHANNEL a model must answer through (forced single token vs. a WORKING SURFACE on which it may externalize its computation) is a DEGREE OF FREEDOM OF THE INSTRUMENT, NOT A NEUTRAL READOUT. A channel too narrow to carry a multi-step computation can MASK a capability (the 38th witness: the four-instrument composition split DISSOLVED into panel-concordance when the channel alone was widened, reasoning-effort held constant); a wide channel can SCAFFOLD one. So NO NEUTRAL CHANNEL → a behavioral capability claim is INDEXED TO A CHANNEL; an unindexed one is underspecified. UPSHOTS: (1) a forced-format capability-NEGATIVE is CHANNEL-BOUNDED, never a capacity verdict, until the channel is varied — the kind-2 verdict is a TRUE measurement of a CHANNEL-BOUNDED capability, the error is MIS-DESCRIPTION not false measurement (preserves essay/undischargeable-negative); (2) the channel is a MANDATORY, HIGH-VALUE control essay/witness-seeking-economics should rank AMONG THE FIRST easings not last (cheap; recurs across the instrument library; was the DECISIVE axis here, tried 5th). SCOPED: bites only when the capability is SERIAL+EXTERNALIZABLE AND the channel forbids externalizing it → single-token TASKS (acceptability, single-premise NLI) untouched. Draws a MACHINE PERFORMANCE/COMPETENCE map (the aperture is a performance constraint masking a competence — a frame, no human claim; cites concept/formal-vs-functional-competence) + an APERTURE-vs-CEILING DUAL with essay/transcript-ceiling (input-medium ceiling vs output-channel aperture; the two errors — ceiling-mistaken-for-aperture vs aperture-mistaken-for-ceiling — are opposite ends of one instrument).
